USA_add_apathy = {
	randomize_temp_variable = {
		var = temp_USA_consumer_apathy
		distribution = uniform
		min = USA_apathy_min
		max = USA_apathy_max
	}
	add_to_variable = { USA_Consumer_Apathy_Var = temp_USA_consumer_apathy }
	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_Consumer_Apathy_Var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_adding_consumer_apathy_tt
}

USA_add_USA_price_concern = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_price_concerns_var = 0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_price_concern_in_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_add_USA_energy_woe = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_energy_woes_var = 0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_energy_woe_in_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_add_USA_business = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_industry_disdain_var = 0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_business_in_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_sub_USA_price_concern = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_price_concerns_var = -0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_price_concern_de_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_sub_USA_energy_woe = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_energy_woes_var = -0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_energy_woe_de_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_sub_USA_business = {
	add_to_variable = { USA_industry_disdain_var = -0.10 }
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_business_de_tt
	USA_unconcerning_boil_over = yes
}

USA_unconcerning_boil_over = {
	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_price_concerns_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_energy_woes_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_industry_disdain_var
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}

	set_temp_variable = { temp_price = USA_price_concerns_var }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_energy = USA_energy_woes_var }
	set_temp_variable = { temp_disdain = USA_industry_disdain_var }

	set_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = 0 }
	set_temp_variable = { one_hundo = 1 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = USA_price_concerns_var }
	add_to_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = USA_energy_woes_var }
	add_to_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = USA_industry_disdain_var }
	add_to_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = USA_unconcerning_thoughts_var }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { TOTAL_AMM > 1 }
		}
		divide_temp_variable = { temp_price = TOTAL_AMM }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp_energy = TOTAL_AMM }
		divide_temp_variable = { temp_disdain = TOTAL_AMM }
		divide_variable = { USA_unconcerning_thoughts_var = TOTAL_AMM }
		set_variable = { USA_price_concerns_var = temp_price }
		set_variable = { USA_energy_woes_var = temp_energy }
		set_variable = { USA_industry_disdain_var = temp_disdain }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { TOTAL_AMM < 1 }
		}
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { TOTAL_AMM = one_hundo }
		divide_temp_variable = { one_hundo = 7 }
		add_to_variable = { USA_price_concerns_var = one_hundo }
		add_to_variable = { USA_price_concerns_var = one_hundo }

		add_to_variable = { USA_energy_woes_var = one_hundo }
		add_to_variable = { USA_energy_woes_var = one_hundo }

		add_to_variable = { USA_industry_disdain_var = one_hundo }
		add_to_variable = { USA_industry_disdain_var = one_hundo }

		add_to_variable = { USA_unconcerning_thoughts_var = one_hundo }
	}
}

## Crime Bill

USA_adjust_cb_support = {

	set_temp_variable = { total_votes = 0 }

	set_temp_variable = { rep_seats = USA_REP_seat_pc_cb }
	set_temp_variable = { dem_seats = USA_DEM_seat_pc_cb }
	set_temp_variable = { pro_seats = USA_PRO_seat_pc_cb }
	set_temp_variable = { nat_seats = USA_NAT_seat_pc_cb }

	multiply_temp_variable = { rep_seats = RD_R_senators }
	multiply_temp_variable = { dem_seats = RD_D_senators }
	multiply_temp_variable = { pro_seats = NPP_C_senators }
	multiply_temp_variable = { nat_seats = NPP_FR_senators }

	round_temp_variable = rep_seats
	round_temp_variable = dem_seats
	round_temp_variable = pro_seats
	round_temp_variable = nat_seats

	set_variable = { USA_R_crimebill_seat_support = rep_seats }
	set_variable = { USA_D_crimebill_seat_support = dem_seats }
	set_variable = { USA_P_crimebill_seat_support = pro_seats }
	set_variable = { USA_N_crimebill_seat_support = nat_seats }

	add_to_temp_variable = { total_votes = USA_R_crimebill_seat_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total_votes = USA_D_crimebill_seat_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total_votes = USA_P_crimebill_seat_support }
	add_to_temp_variable = { total_votes = USA_N_crimebill_seat_support }
	set_variable = { USA_crime_bill_support = total_votes }
}

	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_crime_bill_harsh
		min = 0
		max = 1
	}
	custom_effect_tooltip = USA_add_harsh_cb_tt

		max = 1

USA_change_trust_in_government = {
	set_temp_variable = { tempTrust_tt = tempTrust }
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { tempTrust_tt > 0 } }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_increase_trust_in_government_tt
	}
	else = {
		multiply_temp_variable = { tempTrust_tt = -1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = USA_decrease_trust_in_government_tt
	}
	add_to_variable = { USA_trust_in_government = tempTrust }
	clamp_variable = { var = USA_trust_in_government min = 0 max = 100 }
	USA_calculate_troop_morale = yes
}

USA_calculate_troop_morale = {
	hidden_effect = {
		set_temp_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_temp = USA_trust_in_government }
		set_temp_variable = { USA_optics_temp = USA_optics }
		set_temp_variable = { USA_hawkishness_temp = USA_hawkishness }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_temp = 5 }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_optics_temp = 5 }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_hawkishness_temp = 10 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_temp = USA_optics_temp }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_temp = 2 }
		set_temp_variable = { USA_average_temp = USA_trust_in_government_temp }
		set_temp_variable = { USA_average_temp_2 = USA_trust_in_government_temp }
		multiply_temp_variable = { USA_average_temp_2 = 0.20 }
		subtract_from_temp_variable = { USA_average_temp = USA_average_temp_2 }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_hawkishness_temp = 2 }
		divide_temp_variable = { USA_hawkishness_temp = 7 }
		add_to_temp_variable = { USA_hawkishness_temp = 1 }
		multiply_temp_variable = { USA_average_temp = USA_hawkishness_temp }
		set_variable = { USA_troop_morale = USA_average_temp }
		round_variable = USA_troop_morale
		clamp_variable = {
			var = USA_troop_morale
			min = 1
			max = 100
		}
		USA_calculate_homefront_effects = yes
	}
}

USA_homefront_calculate_manpower_depletion = {
	set_variable = { USA_homefront_total_manpower_depletion = 0 }
	add_to_variable = { USA_homefront_total_manpower_depletion = USA_manpower_depletion_SAW } # South African War
	add_to_variable = { USA_homefront_total_manpower_depletion = USA_manpower_depletion_WAC } # West African Conflict
	add_to_variable = { USA_homefront_total_manpower_depletion = USA_manpower_depletion_COLCW } # Colombian Civil War
	# insert more proxies here

	clamp_variable = {
		var = USA_homefront_total_manpower_depletion
		min = 0
		max = 100
	}
}

#check on extremists so that if they dominate the NPP they get unity
USA_extremist_unity_check = {
	set_temp_variable = { npp_total_pie = party_popularity@communist }
	add_to_temp_variable = { npp_total_pie = party_popularity@national_socialism }
	add_to_temp_variable = { npp_total_pie = party_popularity@paternalism }
	add_to_temp_variable = { npp_total_pie = party_popularity@progressivism }

	set_temp_variable = { commie_dominance = party_popularity@communist }
	multiply_temp_variable = { commie_dominance = 4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { commie_dominance = party_popularity@progressivism }
	divide_temp_variable = { commie_dominance = 4 }
	divide_temp_variable = { commie_dominance = npp_total_pie }

	set_temp_variable = { yockey_dominance = party_popularity@national_socialism }
	multiply_temp_variable = { yockey_dominance = 4 }
	add_to_temp_variable = { yockey_dominance = party_popularity@paternalism }
	divide_temp_variable = { yockey_dominance = 4 }
	divide_temp_variable = { yockey_dominance = npp_total_pie }

	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { party_popularity@national_socialism > 0.14 }
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@communist > 0.14 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance > 0.33 }
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance < 0.50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance > 0.49 }
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance < 0.60 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance > 0.59 }
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance < 0.75 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.40 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { yockey_dominance > 0.74 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.60 }
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { party_popularity@communist > 0.14 }
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { party_popularity@national_socialism > 0.14 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { commie_dominance > 0.33 }
				check_variable = { commie_dominance < 0.50 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { commie_dominance > 0.49 }
				check_variable = { commie_dominance < 0.60 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.25 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { commie_dominance > 0.59 }
				check_variable = { commie_dominance < 0.75 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.40 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { commie_dominance > 0.74 }
			}
			add_to_variable = { USA_NPP_unity = 0.60 }
		}
	}
}

USA_calculate_homefront_effects = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_trust_in_government < 50.99 } }
			set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = 50 }
			set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 50 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = USA_trust_in_government }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = USA_trust_in_government }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 0.1 }
			divide_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = 0.01 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = -1 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_trust_in_government > 50.99 } }
			set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = USA_trust_in_government }
			set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = USA_trust_in_government }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = 0.1 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 0.1 }
			divide_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 5 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc = 0.01 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 = 0.001 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_optics < 50.99 } }
			set_variable = { USA_optics_calc = 50 }
			set_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = 50 }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_optics_calc = USA_optics }
			subtract_from_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = USA_optics }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc = -1 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { USA_optics > 50.99 } }
			set_variable = { USA_optics_calc = USA_optics }
			set_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = USA_optics }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc = 0.001 }
			multiply_variable = { USA_optics_calc_2 = 0.001 }
		}
		set_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc = USA_troop_morale }
		multiply_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc = 0.001 }
		multiply_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc = -1 }

		set_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc_2 = 100 }
		subtract_from_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc_2 = USA_troop_morale }
		multiply_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc_2 = 0.01 }
		multiply_variable = { USA_troop_morale_calc_2 = -1 }

		set_variable = { USA_service_manpower_fufillment_calc = 100 }

	multiply_variable = { pro_floor_val_minority = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { pro_floor_val_proivist = proivist_pro_affiliation }
	multiply_variable = { pro_floor_val_proivist = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { pro_floor_val_urban = urban_pro_affiliation }
	multiply_variable = { pro_floor_val_urban = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { pro_floor_val_rural = rural_pro_affiliation }
	multiply_variable = { pro_floor_val_rural = 0.05 }

	set_variable = { pro_floor_val_union = union_pro_affiliation }
	multiply_variable = { pro_floor_val_union = 0.05 }
}

USA_fopo_improve_breakfront_natspirit = {
	if = {
		limit = { has_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_1 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_1
			add_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_2
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_2 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_2
			add_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_3
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { has_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_3 }
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_3
			add_idea = USA_SAW_breaking_thru_front_4
		}
	}
}

USA_calculate_display_variables = { #If it isn't clear, this is just taking the variables for effects and making them into something the player can see.
	set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_display = USA_trust_in_government_calc }
	multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_display = 100 }
	set_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_display_2 = USA_trust_in_government_calc_2 }
	multiply_variable = { USA_trust_in_government_display_2 = 100 }

	set_variable = { USA_optics_display = USA_optics_calc }
	multiply_variable = { USA_optics_display = 100 }
	set_variable = { USA_optics_display_2 = USA_optics_calc_2 }
	multiply_variable = { USA_optics_display_2 = 100 }

	set_variable = { USA_troop_morale_display = USA_troop_morale_calc }
	multiply_variable = { USA_troop_morale_display = 100 }

	set_variable = { USA_service_manpower_fufillment_display = USA_service_manpower_fufillment_calc }
	multiply_variable = { USA_service_manpower_fufillment_display = 100 }
	set_variable = { USA_service_manpower_fufillment_display_2 = USA_service_manpower_fufillment_calc_2 }
	multiply_variable = { USA_service_manpower_fufillment_display_2 = 100 }
}

USA_fire_succession_event_Schlafly = {
	if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { USA_prev_president = RFK } }
		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.6 days = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { USA_prev_president = WALLACE } }
		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.7 days = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { USA_prev_president = BENNETT } }
		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.8 days = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { check_variable = { USA_prev_president = JOHNSON } }
		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.9 days = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {

		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.10 days = 3 }
	}
	else_if = {

		country_event = { id = USA.succession_letters.11 days = 3 }
	}

USA_check_if_crisis_to_cancel_bill = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = { USA_crisis_counter > 0 }
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					check_variable = { bill_id = 56 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 57 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 58 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 60 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 63 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 64 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 65 }
					check_variable = { bill_id = 66 }
				}
			}
		}
		USA_bill_clear = yes
		clear_variable = bill_id
	}
}
